Critics allege that confidential data acquired by HHS could be exploited by other federal agencies in unregulated and potentially harmful ways.<sup id=\"cite_ref-Albergotti_115-1\" class=\"reference\"><a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Palantir_Technologies#cite_note-Albergotti-115\">[115]</a></sup> Alternative proposals request greater transparency in the process to determine whether any of the data aggregated would be shared with the US Immigration and Customs Enforcement to single out undocumented immigrants.<sup id=\"cite_ref-Albergotti_115-2\" class=\"reference\"><a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Palantir_Technologies#cite_note-Albergotti-115\">[115]</a></sup></p>\r\n<h3><span id=\"Project_Maven_.28since_2018.29\"></span><span id=\"Project_Maven_(since_2018)\" class=\"mw-headline\">Project Maven (since 2018)</span></h3>\r\n<p>After Google had issues with employees walking out concerning the new contract in partnership with the Pentagon, Project Maven, a secret artificial intelligence program aimed at the unmanned operation of aerial vehicles, was taken up by Palantir. Critics warn that the technology could lead to autonomous weapons that decide who to strike without human input.<sup id=\"cite_ref-:0_78-1\" class=\"reference\"><a href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Palantir_Technologies#cite_note-:0-78\">[78]</a></sup></p>\r\n<h2><span id=\"See_also\" class=\"mw-headline\">See also</span></h2>\r\n<ul>\r\n<li><a title=\"Government by algorithm\" href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Government_by_algorithm\">Government by algorithm</a></li>\r\n</ul>\r\n<h2><span id=\"References\" class=\"mw-headline\">References</span></h2>\r\n<div class=\"reflist reflist-columns references-column-width\" style=\"column-width: 30em;\">\r\n<ol class=\"references\">\r\n<li id=\"cite_note-10K-1\"></li>\r\n</ol>\r\n</div>\r\n<ul>\r\n<li id=\"cite_note-10K-1\"><span class=\"reference-text\"><cite class=\"citation web cs1\"><a class=\"external text\" href=\"https://www.sec.gov/ix?doc=/Archives/edgar/data/1321655/000132165523000011/pltr-20221231.htm\" rel=\"nofollow\">\"US SEC: Form 10-K Palantir Technologies Inc\"</a>. <a title=\"U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission\" href=\"https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/U.S._Securities_and_Exchange_Commission\">U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission</a>. 21 February 2023.</cite></span></li>\r\n<li id=\"cite_note-2\"></li>\r\n<li id=\"cite_note-2\"><span class=\"reference-text\"><cite id=\"CITEREFBursztynsky2020\" class=\"citation news cs1\">Bursztynsky, Jessica (19 August 2020). <a class=\"external text\" href=\"https://www.cnbc.com/2020/08/19/palantir-headquarters-moves-from-silicon-valley-to-colorado.html\" rel=\"nofollow\">\"Palantir to relocate headquarters from Silicon Valley to Colorado\"</a>.
